 Following Pakistan's refusal to sever ties with the Haqqani network of militants, a leading US daily has said that the country's military battling the problems is playing a double game of seeking help from the US and supporting the Afghan Taliban
 neuyark times ne ‘‘kripold, caotic pakistan’’ sheershak se sampadakeey main kaha he ki pakistan lambe samay se ugravadiyon ke khilaaf kadi karrwai karne ke obama prashasan ke agrahon kii andekhi karata ja rahaa he
 These militants cross the border and attack US forces deployed in Afghanistan
 isamen kaha gaya he ki haal hi main taliban ugravadiyon ne seemaa paar se hamale kar pakistani sainikon ko maar daalaa or is ghatana ke baad islamabad ko chahie ki vah shikaayat gambhir rup se le
 "there should be a common ground of fighting extremists, but it does not appear that Pakistan's military officials believe it," the editorial said
 unhen yah dekhne kii jarurat he ki afghanistan main failaa ugravad khud unke desh ke liye khatra he or hajaaron pakistani sainik tathaa naagarik isaki bhent chadhe hai
 '' ‘neuyark times’ ne kaha he, ‘‘baharhaal, unhone hakkaani or anya ugravadiyon se sambandh todane se manaa kar diya he jabaki ugravadi is sthiti kaa phayda uthaa rahe hai or desh ko sthir karne ke america ke prayaason ke liye sabase bada khatra bhi hai
 "it says that Pakistan's political system has become dormant while it needs to deal with the border threat rapidly
" sampadakeey main kaha gaya he ki afghanistan main jab tak bharat kii gatividhiyaan paardarshee hai tab tak uski badhati bhoomika myne rakhti he or bhartiya companiyaan yuddh prabhavit desh main nivesh kar rahi hai
 The newspaper wrote that Pakistan could take advantage of the US situation after 2001 which needs help in defeating Al Qaeda and Taliban in Afghanistan
 is tarah pakistan ke paas ek adhik sthir desh ke rup main viksit hone kaa avasar tha
 Pakistan has also taken help of billions of dollars
 ‘‘lekin unki sena lagaataar doharaa khel khel rahi he tathaa raajnneetijna khamosh baithe hai
 On one hand, money was taken from the US and on the other side the Afghan Taliban was helped
 ’’ sampadakeey ke anusaar, ‘‘jald hi badi sankhya main america sainik afghanistan chhod denge or pakistan ko apane shatruon se bachaav karnaa mushkil ho jayega
 '' Comments sampadakeey main aage kaha gaya he ki america congress ke kuch sadsy hakkaani network ko videshi aatankwaadi sanghathan kaa darja dena chaahate hai lekin aisa kadam sahi nahin hoga kyonki isse pakistan ko aatankwaadi desh kaa darja dene kaa rasta ban jayega or use pratibandh kaa saamana karnaa hoga
 Then it will be difficult to cooperate with him
 akhbaar ne likhaa he, ‘‘america ke paas pakistan or uski sena ke saath kaam karne kii koshish ke alaava doosraa vikalp nahin he
 "it is further written that the Obama administration is losing the patience of the officials and the US cannot get away from Pakistan because it needs its help in reopening important supply routes to Afghanistan and urging the Taliban to join the peace talks
" So that by the end of 2014 the troops can be removed from Afghanistan

 Indian batsman Rohit Sharma, who is out of the Test series against England, said on Friday that if the doctors decide to have his injured thigh operation, he will be out of cricket for at least three months
 unhone test team main shaamil kiye gaye olerounder hardik pandya ko kaaphi pratibhashali bataaya
 Rohit told reporters on the sidelines of an event, "I don't know (how long i will be out of cricket), the BCCI medical team is in touch with the doctors, all the scans have been sent to the doctors so far
 , We are awaiting their opinion whether to undergo surgery or not
 agar ham surgery karaate hai to kitne samay kii jarurat hogi
 '' mumbai ke khilaadi ne kaha, ‘‘abhi chijen spasht nahin hai
 i think things will clear up in a day or two whether or not there will be surgery
 agar ham surgery karaate hai to yah ahm faisla hoga
 If i get surgery, i will not be able to play for three or half months
 ham doctoron kii raay kaa intjaar kar rahe hai, dekhie kya hota he
 '' chot kii prakruti ke bare main poochne par rohit sharma ne kaha, ‘‘jaisaa ki aapane dekha, ran lete samay mansapeshiyon main khinchaav aa gaya, tab mujhe laga ki main krij tak nahin pahunch saktaa isaliye main kud gaya

 ’’ He said, "the next two days were Diwali, so all the hospitals were closed, so we got a scan done on November 1 and only after that the medical report was given to the BCCI medical team
 ’’ Asked about the inclusion of all-rounder Hardik Pandya in the Test team, Rohit Sharma said, "we are all waiting
" mujhe ummid he ki use pehla test match mili, yah uske prashansakon, parivaar or doston ke liye acchhee khabar hogi
 Pandya has played under the captaincy of Rohit in Mumbai Indians
 tippaniyan "he has talent, he throws fast balls and he also has the ability to bat in the lower order," he said
 vah rajya kii team ke liye aisa kar chukaa he
 So i don't see any reason why he wouldn't do the same for the national team

 The Supreme Court has given a major verdict on Thursday in the Delhi Government vs Lieutenant Governor (LG) case
 justise eke sikri or justise ashok bhushan kii peeth ne dilli sarkaar ko jhatka dete hue kaha he ki asibi, jaanch aayogon aadi par centre ko adhikaar he
 At the same time, the state government's authority on the circle rate of electricity and land has been stated
 ol india services par adhikaar ko lekar justise sikri or justise ashok bhushan kaa faisla alag rahaa, jis par ab is maamle ko teen jajon kii bench ko bheja jayega
 However, Justice Sikri had stated the central government's authority over the services
 justise sikri nekaha ki aasaani se kaamkaaj ke liye ek maikenism hona chahie
 At the same time, he also said that the lieutenant governor has the right to transfer the level above the joint secretary
 justise sikri ne faisla padhate huekaha ki anti karpshan beuro (asibi) par bhi centre kaa hi adhikaar he
 At the same time, said the authority of the state government on electricity
 justise sikri ne kaha ki jaanch ayog banane kaa adhikaar centre ke paas he
 The Supreme Court said that in case of any difference of opinion, the opinion of the Lieutenant Governor would be considered
 darasal supreme court main daakhil yachikaaon ne maang kii thi ki sevaaon, afasaron ke transfar- posting or anti karpshan beuro, jaanch kamishan ke gathan par kiskaa adhikaar he, isko lekar court chijen spasht kare

 Even if the driving license is not in the pocket, your challan will not be deducted, the condition is just this much
 
 
 mantralay ne haal hi main kendriya motor vaahan niyam 2017 ke masaude par sabhi pakshon se suzav maange hai
 In the proposed rules, two main measures have been taken to deal with the problem of making DL in a fake way
 inamen diel banavaane ke liye kisi manyataprapt motor driving skool ke praaanpatr ko aavedan form ke saath jamaa karne ke alaava nae or maujuuda diel ko aadhaar card se jodne kii anivaaryta ko shaamil kiya gaya he
 Transport expert Anil Chikara, who was among those who drafted the proposed rule, said that linking DL to the 12-digit Aadhaar number would make it easier to create fake licenses and trace more than one DL made from the transport authorities of different states of the same person

 japani bukhaar kii aamad darj hone kii khabar ke baad chhattisgarh ke sukama jile ke darjanon gaanv main viraani chaane lagi he

 is gaanv main sannata chaaya hua he

 kai aise gramin bhi he, jo apane gharon main taala lagaakar jagadalpur, sukama, bijapur, kota, dantewada or kanker main apane naate rishtedaaro ke yahaan sharan liye hue hai
